We had Thanksgiving dinner with 4 of my family members mid-afternoon.  This restaurant is normally very good (classy) but Thanksgiving dinner here was very poor.  They charge $50/head and also add a gratuity (no matter how many in your party).  The food was poor, overcooked, stale rolls. The only thing that was ok was the salmon.  The desert table was a complete joke (embarrassing!).  The deserts looked like they were sitting around for a few days. The staff working during the day were polite but they just didn't seem like they knew how to work in a restaurant.  I think the Nautical Cowboy should never, ever have a Thanksgiving event again....just be closed and stick to your normal menu and hopefully experienced, professionally trained wait-staff. Beautiful water. Tough hikes off the trail. Great spot in Tahoe<//Review>
<Pictures>[{'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipO80qG2WYijIcCuYd2g25TqMJZgy13nJ8n1GOog=w150-h150-k-no-p']}]<//Pictures><resp>None< /resp><gmapID>0x809986614c03badb:0x6f5971a91780f59f<//gmapID></record></dataset><record>
<Gmap_id>0x809986614c03badb:0x6f5971a91780f59f<//Gmap_id><Rate>5</Rate><Response>None<//Response>< review>
it's a big campground, but it's very homey.  The tent spots are far enough from the road to feel secluded, and they offer great views.  There are several hikes within the camp site itself.  There is water provided, along with bathrooms and private showers.  Each site has a fire pit, barbecue, table and benches, and a bear box.  Overall a few pleasant experience and I would definitely come back!</review>

<Text>My wife and I stayed here for a couple days and loved it. The campground was quiet and and clean. There were tons of yellow jackets but they actually emailed us to advise to get a trap for them. Bathrooms are great and there are even trails to the lake, a lookout point, and even to Vikingsholm. I will definitely camp here again. They also have big bundles of wood for campfires ($9) for sale which supports the campsite and the shower tokens are $1 for 3 min< /Text><pictures>None</pictures><Resp>None</Resp>< Gmap_id>

<time>1502604261539</time><Gmap_id>0x80c2c0e7d056df73:0x23c14083a0406da4<//Gmap_id>< Review>
A very well priced buffet. If you're generally a fan of soup then you'll have a good time here. The soups are always good quality, but it is worth checking on thier site to see what soups they have available at the current moment. The salads are good quality for a buffet. The desserts are always excellent, and they have actual soft serve ice cream and not frozen yogurt like most places. If you sign up for thier free online membership program you'll be sent good coupons each week that reduce the price by a fee dollars per person. They do run out of spoons fairly frequently so make sure to let the staff know if they're running low.</Review>

Would rather go to panda express or any of the other places around there. Costco does a much better job and now they take cards too so... btw im complaing about the price haveing gotten coupon to get in.
